\mbox{\Hypertarget{swscale__internal_8h_a045a65065786ad4602ced82aff713230}\label{swscale__internal_8h_a045a65065786ad4602ced82aff713230}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sws_slice}{Sws\+Slice}} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sws_slice}{Sws\+Slice}}}

Struct which defines a slice of an image to be scaled or an output for a scaled slice. A slice can also be used as intermediate ring buffer for scaling steps. \mbox{\Hypertarget{swscale__internal_8h_ad6d098f9400d0f16868e7eb799b6ea58}\label{swscale__internal_8h_ad6d098f9400d0f16868e7eb799b6ea58}} 
\index{swscale\_internal.h@{swscale\_internal.h}!yuv2anyX\_fn@{yuv2anyX\_fn}}
\index{yuv2anyX\_fn@{yuv2anyX\_fn}!swscale\_internal.h@{swscale\_internal.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{yuv2anyX\_fn}{yuv2anyX\_fn}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}}($\ast$ yuv2any\+X\+\_\+fn) (struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sws_context}{Sws\+Context}} $\ast$\mbox{\hyperlink{target__dec__fuzzer_8c_acfe27e61edea06412363421f1a013e81}{c}}, const int16\+\_\+t $\ast$lum\+Filter, const int16\+\_\+t $\ast$$\ast$lum\+Src, \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} lum\+Filter\+Size, const int16\+\_\+t $\ast$chr\+Filter, const int16\+\_\+t $\ast$$\ast$chr\+U\+Src, const int16\+\_\+t $\ast$$\ast$chr\+V\+Src, \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} chr\+Filter\+Size, const int16\+\_\+t $\ast$$\ast$alp\+Src, \mbox{\hyperlink{audio__convert_8c_ae1affc9ca37cfb624959c866a73f83c2}{uint8\+\_\+t}} $\ast$$\ast$dest, \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} dstW, \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} y)}

Write one line of horizontally scaled Y/\+U/\+V/A to Y\+U\+V/\+R\+GB output by doing multi-\/point vertical scaling between input pixels.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & S\+WS scaling context \\
\hline
{\em lum\+Filter} & vertical luma/alpha scaling coefficients, 12 bits \mbox{[}0,4096\mbox{]} \\
\hline
{\em lum\+Src} & scaled luma (Y) source data, 15 bits for 8-\/10-\/bit output, 19 bits for 16-\/bit output (in int32\+\_\+t) \\
\hline
{\em lum\+Filter\+Size} & number of vertical luma/alpha input lines to scale \\
\hline
{\em chr\+Filter} & vertical chroma scaling coefficients, 12 bits \mbox{[}0,4096\mbox{]} \\
\hline
{\em chr\+U\+Src} & scaled chroma (U) source data, 15 bits for 8-\/10-\/bit output, 19 bits for 16-\/bit output (in int32\+\_\+t) \\
\hline

Write one line of horizontally scaled Y/\+U/\+V/A to packed-\/pixel Y\+U\+V/\+R\+GB output without any additional vertical scaling (or point-\/scaling). Note that this function may do chroma scaling, see the \char`\"{}uvalpha\char`\"{} argument.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em c} & S\+WS scaling context \\
\hline
{\em lum\+Src} & scaled luma (Y) source data, 15 bits for 8-\/10-\/bit output, 19 bits for 16-\/bit output (in int32\+\_\+t) \\
\hline
{\em chr\+U\+Src} & scaled chroma (U) source data, 15 bits for 8-\/10-\/bit output, 19 bits for 16-\/bit output (in int32\+\_\+t) \\
\hline
{\em chr\+V\+Src} & scaled chroma (V) source data, 15 bits for 8-\/10-\/bit output, 19 bits for 16-\/bit output (in int32\+\_\+t) \\
\hline
{\em alp\+Src} & scaled alpha (A) source data, 15 bits for 8-\/10-\/bit output, 19 bits for 16-\/bit output (in int32\+\_\+t) \\
\hline
{\em dest} & pointer to the output plane. For 16-\/bit output, this is uint16\+\_\+t \\
\hline
{\em dstW} & width of lum\+Src and alp\+Src in pixels, number of pixels to write into dest\mbox{[}\mbox{]} \\
\hline
{\em uvalpha} & chroma scaling coefficient for the second line of chroma pixels, either 2048 or 0. If 0, one chroma input is used for 2 output pixels (or if the S\+W\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+F\+U\+L\+L\+\_\+\+C\+H\+R\+\_\+\+I\+NT flag is set, it generates 1 output pixel). If 2048, two chroma input pixels should be averaged for 2 output pixels (this only happens if S\+W\+S\+\_\+\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+F\+U\+L\+L\+\_\+\+C\+H\+R\+\_\+\+I\+NT is not set) \\
\hline
{\em y} & vertical line number for this output. This does not need to be used to calculate the offset in the destination, but can be used to generate comfort noise using dithering for some output formats. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_sws_context}{Sws\+Context}}$\ast$ sws\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+set\+\_\+opts (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{srcW,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{srcH,  }\item[{enum \mbox{\hyperlink{pixfmt_8h_a9a8e335cf3be472042bc9f0cf80cd4c5}{A\+V\+Pixel\+Format}}}]{src\+Format,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{dstW,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{dstH,  }\item[{enum \mbox{\hyperlink{pixfmt_8h_a9a8e335cf3be472042bc9f0cf80cd4c5}{A\+V\+Pixel\+Format}}}]{dst\+Format,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{flags,  }\item[{const double $\ast$}]{param }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}
